implements a comprehensive dashboard JSON schema version migration system spanning both backend (Go) and frontend (TypeScript) components. The pipeline consists of 41 sequential schema migrations (v2 through v42) that transform legacy dashboards to the current schema while maintaining backward compatibility.\\n\\n### Backend Migration System (apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/)\\n\\n#### Migration Runner\\nThe core migration orchestrator is implemented in `apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/migrate.go`. The `Initialize()` function sets up a singleton migrator instance that holds the complete version-to-function mapping. The `Migrate()` function executes sequential migrations on a dashboard object, tracking schema version progression from the input version to a target version (default: v42).\\n\\nThe migrator performs the following operations in sequence:\\n1. Cleans up backend-specific properties not present in frontend saves\\n2. Tracks original transformations and field configs for property preservation\\n3. Applies frontend defaults to replicate frontend initialization behavior\\n4. Ensures all panels have unique IDs\\n5. Executes versioned migrations sequentially\\n6. Adds built-in annotation query\\n7. Cleans up dashboard properties for save compatibility\\n\\n#### Versioned Migration Registry\\nThe migration registry is centralized in `apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/schemaversion/migrations.go`. The `GetMigrations()` function returns a map[int]SchemaVersionMigrationFunc where each version number maps to a migration function. This registry implements a factory pattern that binds data source providers to migrations that require them (V33 and V36). The schema version range spans from v2 through v42 (minimum supported is v13, latest is v42).\\n\\nThe registry uses the type `SchemaVersionMigrationFunc` defined as: `func(context.Context, map[string]interface{}) error`. Most migrations are simple stateless functions, while V33 and V36 return closures that capture the DataSourceInfoProvider for datasource resolution.\\n\\n#### Individual Migration Steps\\nAll individual migration implementations follow the pattern of versioned Go files (v2.go through v42.go) in the schemaversion package. Key migrations include:\\n\\n- **V2**: Migrates legacy services.filter structure to top-level templating and time properties\\n- **V6**: Moves drop-downs to new annotation schema and converts template variables from 'filter' type to 'query'\\n- **V7**: Migrates nav structure to timepicker\\n- **V16**: Performs grid layout migration from row-based to grid-based layout system (major structural change)\\n- **V23**: Updates template variable handling\\n- **V24**: Migrates table panels with timeseries-to-rows transformations\\n- **V31**: Handles labels-to-fields transformer migration\\n- **V33**: Migrates datasource references with DataSourceInfoProvider lookup\\n- **V36**: Transforms datasource references from string format to structured UID-based objects with type and apiVersion\\n- **V38**: Migrates table cell options and display modes\\n- **V40**: Ensures refresh property is string type\\n- **V41-V42**: Final schema evolution steps\\n\\n#### Support Infrastructure\\n`apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/schemaversion/migration_utils.go` provides utility functions for type-safe data access: `GetStringValue()`, `GetBoolValue()`, `GetIntValue()`, `GetFloatValue()`, and type conversion functions. These utilities mirror frontend type coercion behavior.\\n\\n`apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/schemaversion/datasource_utils.go` handles datasource reference resolution, converting datasource names to UID-based DataSourceRef objects.\\n\\n`apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/schemaversion/errors.go` defines `MigrationError` and `MinimumVersionError` types for structured error reporting.\\n\\n`apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/frontend_defaults.go` replicates frontend DashboardModel and PanelModel default initialization behavior, ensuring backend migrations apply the same defaults the frontend would apply during model construction.\\n\\n`apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/metrics.go` instruments migrations with Prometheus metrics for observability.\\n\\n### Frontend Migration System (public/app/features/dashboard/state/)\\n\\n#### DashboardMigrator TypeScript Class\\nThe frontend implementation mirrors backend logic in `public/app/features/dashboard/state/DashboardMigrator.ts`. The class exports `DASHBOARD_SCHEMA_VERSION = 42` as the target version and implements the `updateSchema()` method. This method contains conditional migration blocks that execute based on version ranges (e.g., `if (oldVersion < 16 && finalTargetVersion >= 16)`), allowing targeted migrations that skip intermediate versions when a dashboard is already at a higher version.\\n\\nThe TypeScript implementation handles:\\n- Legacy services.filter migration (v2)\\n- Pulldown/annotation structure migration (v6)\\n- Timepicker migration from nav (v7)\\n- InfluxDB query schema migrations (v8)\\n- Row-to-grid layout migration (v16) with complex panel dimension calculations\\n- Template variable migrations (v23, v27)\\n- Table panel migrations (v24)\\n- Datasource reference transformations (v33, v36)\\n- Panel type auto-migrations for deprecated types\\n\\n#### Integration with DashboardModel\\nThe `public/app/features/dashboard/state/DashboardModel.ts` constructor integrates schema migration by calling `updateSchema()` during initialization. The DashboardModel accepts a `targetSchemaVersion` option to support single-version migrations for testing, defaulting to the latest `DASHBOARD_SCHEMA_VERSION`.\\n\\n### Testing and Validation\\n\\n#### Backend Tests\\nTest files exist for each migration step (v2_test.go through v42_test.go) in the schemaversion package, validating individual migration behavior with JSON fixtures.\\n\\n#### Frontend Tests\\nMultiple test files validate frontend migration consistency:\\n- `DashboardMigrator.test.ts`: Unit tests for individual schema migration logic\\n- `DashboardMigratorToBackend.test.ts`: Comparison tests that verify backend and frontend migrations produce identical results by running curated test dashboards through both pipelines\\n- `DashboardMigratorSingleVersion.test.ts`: Tests single-version migrations (e.g., v15→v16)\\n- `DashboardMigratorToBackend.devDashboards.test.ts`: Tests dev dashboard migrations with full datasource resolution\\n\\nThese tests ensure consistency between frontend and backend migration logic, using test data fixtures in `apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/testdata/input/` and comparing outputs against expected results in `testdata/output/`.\\n\\n### Migration Execution Flow\\n\\n1. **Backend Path**: Dashboard JSON → Backend migration.Migrate() → Apply all schema migrations (v0-v42) → Output v42 JSON\\n2. **Frontend Path**: Dashboard JSON → DashboardModel constructor → DashboardMigrator.updateSchema() → Apply schema migrations → PanelModel creation → Output v42 dashboard object\\n\\nThe system maintains strict backward compatibility by supporting all historical schema versions and enforcing sequential migration execution.
